New Plans for Daxia Middle School 163

Many Aspects Worth Learning From

Daxia Middle School in this city is a complete middle school affiliated with Daxia University, divided into junior and senior high school sections. The senior high school section is divided into three departments: general studies, normal school, and business. The school's educational management facilities have always been well-known and perfect. It is said that they will become even more general in the autumn semester and there are many aspects worth learning from. Below is the letter from the school to the students' parents: Dear Parents, We are writing to you to inform you of the school's facilities for the progress of the students' studies and the cultivation and forging of their minds and bodies. We feel that it is necessary to notify you of the school's facilities at any time, and we sincerely hope that we can get your full cooperation because of this. It is not only the good fortune of one school and one family. Here are the current situation of the school and the decisions that have been decided to be implemented after the autumn semester for your review: 1. School Buildings and Equipment. Our school originally rented houses on Gordon Road as school buildings. Although the school officials have done their best to open the school for five years, the results are still satisfactory, but the junior and senior high schools are not in the same place, and the school area is also cramped. As a result, teaching and guidance have not been as ideal as possible. The university department has now purchased nearly 200 acres of land in Fanwangdu and built its own school buildings, which will be moved after the summer. The remaining Jiaozhou Road school buildings, classrooms, auditoriums, libraries, dormitories for male and female students, sports fields, and all other equipment will be completely moved to this middle school for use. The university department originally had more than 1,400 male and female students. Now, the school buildings and equipment for more than 1,400 people will be moved to this school for use, which will be more spacious than the original equipment of our school. Since our school was opened five years ago, it was officially registered by the Shanghai Special City Education Bureau last spring and was approved by the Education Department and the Shanghai Special Municipal Government for record-keeping. The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has determined that the school's education and management are serious and the content is rich. It has decided to provide subsidies from the 19th year to expand the government's intention to cultivate talents. 2. Teaching. Our school firmly believes that teaching and learning have a very close relationship. Although the achievement of personal academic knowledge depends on the degree of personal effort, the induction of interest in effort and the guidance of learning methods cannot but be the responsibility of the teachers. The improvement of students' grades is not only a negative sanction for declining students, but also a guidance for all students to automatically know what to work hard on. This point, our school has always paid attention to it. At the time of the beginning of the academic year, we decided to hire teachers and staff who are both knowledgeable and experienced and who are brave enough to take responsibility to take charge of the teaching of each subject and the duties of each department. When all the teachers and staff are decided, we will report their names, origins, and experiences to the parents regarding the teaching affairs or duties they are in charge of at the school. Our school not only hopes that there will be a considerable understanding between the school and the family, but also hopes that the teachers and staff and all parents will have a considerable understanding. This will be of great help to the school's teaching management. Regarding academic examinations, our school has always attached great importance to the monthly and semester examination reports, which will still be directly mailed to your parents. Please pay attention to your children's academic performance at school here. If you do not receive the academic performance report, please notify our school immediately and attach the detailed mailing address. If your parents change the mailing address, please notify the school at any time. After the autumn semester starts, our school will implement a self-study room system and force students to exercise after class. It is now scheduled that all student dormitories will be locked by the Moral Education Department from 8:00 AM to 9:00 PM every day except Sundays and holidays. Each tutor and teacher of each subject will guide the students to study in the self-study room. From 4:00 PM to 6:00 PM every afternoon is the time for students to exercise after class. Students must go to the sports field to exercise. Our school has hired physical education instructors to be responsible for guiding everything, so that students can have the opportunity to fully develop both academically and physically. 3. Moral Education. Our school will make the training and guidance of students' lives more reasonable and strict in the future, in order to cultivate energetic and orderly youths. Male and female student dormitories have always been separated in our school. The university department built a female student dormitory on the west side of the school last year, which can accommodate nearly 100 female students, and is now fully used by our school. It is the most concerned thing for the parents and school officials to guide whether the female students are healthy or not at school. Our school has specially hired a doctor with rich knowledge and experience as a health instructor. All students will have a health checkup once a month, and the results of the checkup will be filled out in each student's health report and mailed directly to each parent every month along with the academic performance report. Here, please pay attention to your children's health at school. If you do not receive it, please notify our school immediately. Starting from the autumn semester of this year, male and female students must wear school uniforms. Each student must prepare at least two sets of summer school uniforms and one set of winter school uniforms. The quality, color, and style must be consistent. The cost of this school uniform is about 20 yuan. The surplus will be returned and the deficit will be made up. Shanghai is prosperous. Our school students have also decided to wear school uniforms, so please do not let your children bring gorgeous clothes to school. It is not necessary to bring other valuables to avoid accidents. Our school estimates the highest and lowest amount of living expenses for male and female students as follows. I hope your parents will pay attention. If you want to avoid your children wasting money, you can deposit the expenses for one semester at the school. The school will give them to your children in installments as ordered.

Tuition Fee: Minimum 25 yuan per semester, Maximum 30 yuan per semester; Accommodation Fee: 20 yuan, 20 yuan; Meal Fee: 30 yuan, 35 yuan; Miscellaneous Fee: 15 yuan, 25 yuan; Book Fee: 5 yuan, 25 yuan; Pocket Money: 15 yuan, 30 yuan; Total: 110 yuan, 165 yuan; Remarks: All new and old students of our school must wear uniforms from this semester. In addition to the above expenses, they must pay an additional 20 yuan for uniforms. After that, old students will be exempt from this fee. 4. In addition, in addition to the school's guidance on the further education and employment of graduates, the school is very willing to fulfill the responsibility of investigation and introduction if your parents need special help from the school. In addition, if you want to be stricter in the management of your children or want to focus more on a certain subject, you can also state the reasons in detail at any time, and the school can consider it. After a relative amount of time, the results can be reported to the parents. We hope that your parents will pay close attention to the above points and cooperate with the school. Principal Wang Boqun and Director Ni Wenya of Daxia Middle School affiliated with Daxia University.

Free Talk

A Word or Two Long 170

A person can do things as slowly as a clock. But it should be as accurate as a clock.

Young men admire young women. Old men also admire young women. When demand exceeds supply, their value will naturally increase. But their danger is also greater.

Beautiful women really have short lives. Ugly women often have scandals.

It is better to be ugly and virtuous than beautiful and dissolute.

When men and women seek mates, talent and virtue should be the prerequisites, not wealth and appearance.

People who are full and warm and have nothing to do may do more evil than people who are hungry and cold.

Talking to old people, you can always gain some knowledge. Associating with young girls, it is inevitable that people will criticize you.

Compatriots do not suffer from too low a level of literacy, but from too high a degree of love for foreign goods.

Chinese people only know how to imitate, not to create. Therefore, all kinds of undertakings have no progress.

Medical doctors can examine the strength of the body, but cannot examine the good and evil of the human heart. It is a flaw.

Human beings have no contentment, and the world has no peace.

Ancient gentlemen valued few words and diligence. New figures value lofty talk and rhetoric.

Special Notes on the Chinese Youth Asia Walking Group Zhao·Ding·Ming 171

The Chinese Youth Asia Walking Group has been on the road for a month since it set off. What is the progress? I think this is what those who are interested in the walking business want to hear. So I collected what I heard and saw, and recorded it in a miscellaneous way.

Looking back, the group set off at about 4 p.m. on the 28th of last month. Suddenly, there was a downpour. They happened to be at Longhua. It was as if God was testing their determination. At the beginning of their journey, being drenched by the heavy rain could temper their skills and express their firm will. So they still moved forward in the rain. They camped overnight in the fields near Xinzhuang. They set off at 5 a.m. the next morning. In a few days, they walked to Hangzhou. Because they left Shanghai in a hurry, they did not have time to get their passports. So they submitted a request to the Zhejiang Provincial Government to get them, so as to conduct a survey of the living conditions in various places. However, the Zhejiang Provincial Government believed that it was the proper procedure to obtain a passport at the place of departure. In the future, the provinces and cities that the group travels to should sign and confirm and give them protection. So the group elected the liaison officer Huang Yuejun to return to Shanghai overnight to apply for a passport from the Shanghai Municipal Government. The next day, the Shanghai Municipal Government approved the request. Huang took a document and returned to Hangzhou to report the order. After asking the Zhejiang Provincial Government to sign, he went forward again. Huang once asked me to draft a document and talked to me a few words. Only then did I know that he had this twist.

Recently, I met the so-called liaison doctor Huang Jingwan. I was able to see the reply letter sent by the group from Ningbo, and attached the words of congratulations from various celebrities before departure. I will record them here.

Forward (Yu Youren) Safe journey (Shanghai Jingwu Sports Association) Strong and unceasing (Hangzhou Yousheng Travel Association Branch) Unity of knowledge and action (Lin Jing) Courageous and diligent (Ye Gongchuo) No distance is too far (Zhang Renjie) Thousands of miles of travel (Huang Wan) A great man takes the world as his home (Chen Liting) Reading ten thousand books is not as good as traveling ten thousand miles. (Ge Gongzhen) Don’t worry about having few acquaintances on the road. Remember that brothers are everywhere. (Huang Jingwan) Aim high. Be down-to-earth. See and hear more. Return to your comrades. (Cai Yuanpei)

Ming noted that the group’s souvenirs (inscriptions) are not as complete as those of the National Walking Group. The National Walking Group’s signatures are written on a bundle of lightweight and glossy domestic white silk. It is convenient to carry and quite elegant. It is a complete whole. After returning in five years, the exhibits are displayed and nothing is missed. The group uses horizontal banners and hanging scrolls. Although there are many celebrities and literati who inscribe words everywhere, the paper shafts are heavy and inconvenient to carry, and they are fragmented and easily lost. I hope that the Asia Walking Group can adopt the National Walking Group’s inscription method.

Su Dongpo Smoked Opium Lao·Nu· 172

Most poets of the past were famous for drinking. For example, Li Taibai's "A hundred poems with a bucket of wine" is especially popular. Su Dongpo's reputation as a poet is no less than that of Taibai. For example, in the Ode to the Red Cliff, "I have a bucket of wine, which I have stored for a long time." It is well known that Su Dongpo eats wine and can write poems when climbing high. I am not talking about Su Dongpo's drinking and writing poems now, but about Su Dongpo being a secret opium smoker. Isn't it a big joke to be a regular customer of Swallow's Nest? However, there is no evidence for empty talk. I have poems to prove it.

"Taoist persuades to drink chicken Su water. Boy can make poppy soup". Isn't this Su Dongpo's poem? Isn't this Su Dongpo's poem about smoking opium?

Some people say, "This is not right. If you say that poppy soup is the current opium, then 'chicken Su water' can also be said to be soda made with soda." I said, "I dare not say whether chicken Su water is soda made with soda. But it is well known that opium is made from poppy flowers. It is like the rice we eat, which is made from rice. Speaking of different names, there are various other names such as Champa jade rice. As for when opium was introduced into China, there is no clear record in history. Only in the fourth year of the Song Dynasty's Kaibao period, the Arabs and Guangzhou and Mingzhou (now Ningbo) traded with each other. Among their medicines, there was a kind of 'Mi Nang Flower', which was said to be a substance that calms the mind, increases appetite, and makes people sleep more. Later, Emperor Shenzong of the Ming Dynasty lived in seclusion in the Leopard Room for many years and never went to court. It is said that the 'Yanling Dan' he took was 'opium'." But I found a definite proof in the Piye Law. The method of taking medicine recorded in the law is the current crude opium lamp. And the word 㽼 is especially a major disease for smokers. It is said in Buddhism that Vimalakirti was the first person to smoke opium. Emperor Shenzong of the Ming Dynasty was also a famous opium smoker. Su Dongpo even called a boy to make poppy soup. The elegance is profound. The demeanor of a famous scholar. It is a good story to pass on. It can be used to defend the people in the black list. Because all the people who describe smoking have always been described as ghosts. Now, it is even more in violation of the law. Heavy punishments are used to supervise and punish them.

I also found a kind of evidence. Lin Zexu was a person with a great opium addiction. Because he was determined to quit smoking, the Lin Zexu ointment and pills sold in various pharmacies now are a fact that he set an example. And the Mi Nang Flower ointment produced in Meishan, Sichuan is Su Dongpo's legacy. However, Mi Nang Flower ointment and poppy soup may not be the same thing. How to eat them is probably not with the bamboo spear made by Vimalakirti, nor the Yanling Dan of Emperor Shenzong of the Ming Dynasty.

Billiard Chat Chun·Chao· 173

Billiards is a kind of ball game. Its Western name is Billiard. It has been quite popular in China recently. Because its playing method is simple and clean, it has a kind of mechanical interest. People in the intellectual class like it very much. Ordinary people also like its simplicity and unadornedness. It is not like learning Go, where there are many rules to understand first.

The way to play billiards is very simple. There are four balls on the table. Two red and two white. The white one is called the cue ball. The red one is called the object ball. It is played by two people together. (Although there are three or four people playing together, it is not very common). Each person recognizes one cue ball. Then serve the ball. You must use the cue to hit the cue ball. If the cue ball touches the other two balls continuously, you score points. Touching two red and one white is 5 points. Touching two red is 3 points. Touching one red and one white is 2 points. Touching only one ball has no points.

Ordinary people who learn this game can score 160 to 200 points per hour with one month of effort. The sections (billiard rooms) are usually 40 points each. So it is not difficult for beginners to score 4 or 5 sections in one hour. When I was in Shanghai, I saw a Chinese man and a Western man playing this game in the Datong Hotel. The Western man once scored more than 200 points in a row with one shot. The onlookers were like a wall. After an hour, the Western man won by scoring 22 sections. At that time, I was quite surprised and thought it was a wonderful skill. Later, I heard people say that this is not surprising. In Europe and the United States, some people can score more than 1,000 points in a row with each shot. Compared to this, it is still far behind.

Recently, the business of billiard rooms in Beijing has been very prosperous. There are Huayuan, Huaiyuan, Quanan, Yuyuan, Dongyuan and other shops. Among them, only Huayuan's layout is acceptable. The rest are very simple. The tables, cues and balls are not top-notch. In addition, the Central Hotel and the Youth Association also have billiard rooms attached. The rent is not cheap. It costs 4 or 5 small silver dollars per hour. Dongyuan's rent is less than other shops because the location of the furniture is backward, but the customers are not very enthusiastic.

The Beijing Municipal Authorities once held a city-wide billiard competition. The champion was a man surnamed Shao. It is said that he can score 12 sections per hour. Recently, a waiter named Agou from Shanghai came to the Huaiyuan billiard room. He is from Shanghai. He played with Shao. Shao could not win. Agou had to give him half the points. It is a pity that he came to Beijing a little late. Otherwise, the championship would not have belonged to Shao.

Heart Warmth (245) Bao·Tian·Xiao· 174

Chapter 13: Who Plants Fortune Unintentionally Finds the Ring Only This Fate Heartfully Sings the Golden Thread

At this time, they were very puzzled. Zuo Shichen said, "I clearly remember that after taking it from Shi Guanping's place that day, I stuffed it into my long gown pocket. When the long gown was taken to be washed, it shouldn't have been taken out." His wife said, "Every time I wash clothes, I always take out everything in the pockets and put them in the drawer of your desk. I have never thrown away many things that I know are useless. I let you check them yourself. Now, there are exactly ten coupons. How could I not have noticed them and carelessly thrown them away?" Zuo Shichen said, "There's no way to find it. I'll have to tell Mr. Shi Guanping and wait until I find it before I can claim the prize." At this moment, one of Zuo Shichen's daughters, named Qing'er, who was only five years old, said, "I saw several green pieces of paper in Dad's wallet. What kind of tickets are they?" Her mother asked Zuo Shichen, "Where's your wallet?" Zuo Shichen said, "The wallet is naturally with me." His wife said, "Then Aqing said you have green tickets with you. Is it that coupon? Do you know what color that coupon is?" Zuo Shichen was reminded by her words and changed his mind. He took out the wallet from his side and looked at it. Weren't the ten Plant Fortune coupons safely in the wallet? It turned out that when Shi Guanping gave them to him, he did stuff them into his long gown pocket. Later, when he took off his long gown to work, he probably instinctively feared losing them, so he moved the things in his pockets to the wallet. But he only remembered the first time he stuffed them into his long gown pocket and forgot the second time he moved them from the long gown pocket to the wallet. If he had known this, he would have been searching for them at home. Zuo Shichen couldn't help but laugh at himself. He could really be considered a common man disturbing himself. His wife said, "Isn't that right? You hid them well in your wallet, but you came back and rummaged through them, making people search until they were covered in sweat. And they haven't made any money yet, and they have already made people's heads dizzy. It can be seen that it is not a good thing." Zuo Shichen said, "It's good to find them. Otherwise, after a busy search, they still haven't been found. If the second prize is drawn on these coupons, wouldn't that make people even more frustrated?" At this time, Zuo Shichen, after finding the Plant Fortune coupons, hurriedly took a horse-drawn carriage to Weichun Garden. Shi Guanping said, "I have already investigated. The second prize is indeed in your ten coupons." Zuo Shichen handed the ten coupons to Shi Guanping. The ten were a series of numbers. Shi Guanping counted to the third one and said, "It's here." You can take the prize back. They are going to dismantle this showroom today. We can conclude the matter about the Plant Fortune coupons. The most annoying thing about fundraising is the delay, because everyone has different jobs. This is extra work. A delay often leads to delays in sorting out.

Eastern Tour Shadows (99) Qian·Hua· 175

(95) The Autographing Craze of Athletes

In recent years, as a result of Japan's special promotion of sports, the status of athletes has suddenly increased. Each company and society regards it as an honor to recruit famous athletes. The treatment is extremely good. Their ability to handle affairs is not questioned. For example, Hitomi Kinuko, a world-famous female athlete, was hired by the Osaka Mainichi Newspaper this year as a sports reporter. Her monthly salary is 500 yen per day. She does nothing all day long. Also, Takaisi Katsuo, Japan's top short-distance swimmer, was recently hired by Mitsubishi Corporation as a senior employee. There are many similar examples. People from all walks of life, based on the psychology of worshiping heroes, regard it as an honor to see the faces of athletes. Women are especially fond of it. Their ideal husband is one who is tall and burly, runs like the wind, and occupies a considerable position in the sports world. The beauty or ugliness of his appearance and the black or white of his skin are not taken into account. From the opening day of this year's Far Eastern Games until May 30, athletes from the three countries were surrounded by crowds every day asking for autographs. This can be said to be a new aspect of the conference. In Japan, the autographing craze of athletes is in full swing. The reporter once asked people in the Japanese sports world about the origin of the autographing craze. The exact date cannot be verified. It is only known that it was discovered during the Japan-Germany Sports Games last year. Since then, this trend has gradually become more popular. Until today, several days before the opening of the First Far Eastern Games, athletes from the three countries stayed together at the Japan Youth Hall. The Japanese athletes took the lead and used a pocket-sized diary to ask the Chinese and Filipino athletes to sign their names as a souvenir. Before long, our country's athletes also followed suit. Tang Baokun and Wang Xiliang, the generals of the basketball team, first asked the reporter to sign their names. Turning over their small books, there were already hundreds of signatures. Chinese, English and Japanese were all mixed together. They were carefully treasured and regarded as precious jade. After the opening, dozens or hundreds of Japanese male and female students and elementary school students scattered at the entrances of each stadium and in front of the Youth Hall, asking athletes to sign their names. There were always elementary school students around the age of ten holding broken pieces of paper and crowding in front of the athletes, asking them to write their names loudly. The situation was quite amusing. From May 16, various photos of the conference, commemorative postcards, and commemorative fans were sold in front of the Youth Hall. The craze for autographs became more intense. People were looking for the athletes themselves to sign their names on their own photos. Even the conference staff and overseas Chinese could not escape the custom. The front of the door was crowded with people. The road was blocked. They were all crowds asking for autographs. The famous Ms. Sun Guiyun, Liu Jingzhen, Huang Shufang, Gao Zi and other ladies were even more noticed by the general public. The number of times they were surrounded was also the most. At first, Sun Guiyun did not easily sign autographs for people. Once, a certain student studying abroad held a commemorative fan and asked Sun to sign it. Sun looked at him coldly and said, "What is the meaning of your actions?" The student was embarrassed and could not answer. So he stopped. The next day, Zhang Yongjing, a cadre of the Youth Association, also asked Sun to sign a photo. Sun thought that Zhang had been in charge of the reception for a long time and had worked hard, so she nodded in agreement. But she said that this was actually the first time she had ever signed an autograph. The onlookers heard this and asked her to sign their names one after another. Under heavy siege, Sun had no way to refuse. So she held a pen and wrote freely, responding to each request one by one. In a short time, she signed her name dozens of times. It was also an interesting story in the autographing craze. As a result, the athletes' actions were greatly inconvenienced. The traffic in front of the Youth Hall could not be maintained. After discussion by the cadres of the Sports Association, a strict order was issued on the morning of May 28 to prohibit athletes from signing autographs. A large notice was also posted in front of the Youth Hall, writing the ten characters "Requesting athletes to sign autographs is absolutely not allowed." For a time, this trend was slightly suppressed. But it was still found near the Outer Garden of the Meiji Shrine. It is because this kind of fashion has been deeply imprinted in the minds of the Japanese people and cannot be shaken. Once, the reporter accompanied Zhang Yongjing, a cadre of the Youth Association, to a banquet hosted by a Japanese friend. More than a dozen geishas were invited to the banquet. For a time, there was powder and flowers, the songs of swallows and orioles, soft singing, and laughter filled the room. The Japanese friend jokingly said that the reporter was a sprinter of the Chinese athletes' delegation and Zhang was a high jump master. Before he finished speaking, all the beauties arrived. Zhang was tall and had long legs. Everyone measured him with their jade hands and said, "Indeed, he is a high jumping genius." They took out their bone fans and handkerchiefs and asked us to sign our names. For a time, we were unable to defend ourselves and reluctantly scribbled. The crowd happily dispersed and sat down. Thinking back to this scene and this situation, I can't help but laugh.

Grains: Foreign Rice Suddenly Rises by 3-4 Jiao in the Afternoon 186

Various Groups Compete for 15,000 Bags

Yesterday, foreign rice sales were sluggish in the morning, and the market was weak. Only 3-4,000 bags of each type of rice were opened, and everyone was bearish. In the afternoon, the inland groups from Hangzhou, Shaoxing, and Xiashi, as well as the Yantai group, began to load medium-grade and lower-grade goods. Although the Hankou group returned a large amount of low-grade rice, they slightly loaded nearly 1,000 bags of No. 1 Saigon rice yesterday. Various groups competed for it, and the market price immediately rose by 3-4 jiao. The transaction volume also increased. A total of 14,000-15,000 bags were opened in the market, with the afternoon accounting for 70%. If various customer groups continue to order tomorrow or the day after, the market will definitely stabilize. Small broken rice and coarse rice saw the most transactions yesterday, totaling 5,000 bags, priced at 11 yuan 7 jiao to 10 yuan 7 jiao and a half. Gai rice had 3,500 bags, priced at 14 yuan 3 jiao to 13 yuan 9 jiao and a half. Large broken rice had 3,000 bags, priced at 12 yuan 3 jiao to 11 yuan 8 jiao and a half. Small broken rice had 1,000 bags, priced at 14 yuan 4 jiao to 2 jiao. No. 1 Saigon rice had 1,000 bags, priced at 16 yuan 6 jiao to 4 jiao and a half. No. 2 had 500 bags, priced at 13 yuan 1 jiao and a half. Min Dang rice had 300 bags, priced at 14 yuan 9 jiao and a half. Xu Ye coarse rice had 200 bags, priced at 12 yuan 4 jiao, it was said.

The Process of Flour Settlement in July 187

80,000 Bags Delivered via Warehouse Receipts

Yesterday was the last day for the settlement of standard flour for July. The actual delivery by various factories included 68,000 bags of Red and Blue Car brands from Fufeng and Yutong, 4,000 bags of Green Three Stars brand from Zhonghua, and 8,000 bags of Green Eagle Ball brand from Tailong, for a total of 80,000 bags. It is said that this type of warehouse receipt delivery is partly due to poor customer sales and concerns about the accumulation of spot goods, and partly because prices were raised too high, making delivery necessary. As for those who took delivery, it is said that they were certain customers. However, with sales to the north suspended and distribution difficult, they may suffer some losses in the future. The transaction volume of futures was significantly lower than in June, totaling 7,741,000 bags.

Oil Market: Hankou Rapeseed Oil's Rising Trend Is Strong 188

Highest Price Since the European War

Rapeseed oil sales always peak in the summer because candle production stops and it is exclusively supplied to soap factories. In the past, when our country did not have soap factories, summer was considered a slow period. Since the advent of soap factories, although candle production stopped due to the hot weather, oil sales were not sluggish. This is also a history of market changes. In recent years, soap usage has increased daily, causing summer business to be more prosperous. This year, the winter rapeseed harvest was poor, resulting in a sharp decrease in production. After the start of summer, foreign firms in Hankou and Shanghai have been buying in large quantities, resulting in a state of scarcity. The Hankou telegram the day before stated that soap factories had bought several hundred dan of Macheng oil at a price of 17 taels 2 qian, while Shanghai firms had bought at 17 taels. Today, a detailed letter states that Jingzhi and Jin areas are out of stock. Macheng oil has risen to 17 taels 8 qian, and there is not much stock left. Further purchases may require over 18 taels. This is the highest price since the European War, it is said.

Textiles: Textile Market Becomes Quiet After Changsha Stops Loading 189

Textile transactions returned to quiet yesterday, mainly because the ports in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River are once again unsettled. The Changsha group sent a telegram to stop loading. The Hankou, Shashi, and Jiujiang groups are also waiting and watching, so there were not many transactions yesterday. The street is in a slow period and is even more lifeless. Cloth prices have been significantly affected. The Yuehua velvet from the Eastern goods has already shown signs of turning from rising to falling. Fine serge in dark colors from Tingyi is softening. Cotton French velvet is also down by 2.5 li. Concubine-colored Yang Guifei has been sold for 1 qian 7 fen, and Bird Beauty's large red is 1 qian 8 fen 2 li and a half. The Shuilang velvet, in which the Sichuan group was unusually active, also fell yesterday, with Shuanglong at 2 qian 1 fen, Jiaoye Tishu at 2 qian 5 li, and Yang Guifei at 2 qian 7 li and a half. Only bleached cloth is still firm, with Tiansi Golden at 9 taels 1 qian, Fushou Three Stars at 9 taels 5 qian and a half, and Western Queen Mother at 11 taels 5 qian. Western goods have been in a state of transition recently. Summer goods have reached the end of their season. Autumn goods, after being lively for a while, have become quiet again, so there were not many transactions yesterday, it was said.

Dried Goods: New Orchid Bamboo Branches Arrive in Increasing Quantities 190

New orchid bamboo branches produced in Zhangzhou had a poor harvest this year, and very little arrived after the market opened. Therefore, the previous price had opened as high as 29 taels. Yesterday, the Taikoo Company's Jinan ship arrived from Xiamen, with a total of over 400 boxes, of which orchid bamboo branches accounted for more than half. The increase compared to before is sudden, and the market price is expected to ease slightly. However, land prices are still firm. It is expected that trading can begin tomorrow, it is said.

Yunnan Dried Vegetables: Low Inventory, Short Supply 191

Pickled Mustard Tuber Supply Not Continuing

Yunnan large-headed mustard tuber has not arrived for a long time, and market inventory is quite scarce. The current market price is 48 yuan, and most shops have no stock to sell. Sichuan pickled mustard tuber is also unable to be supplied due to obstructed supply lines. The customer inventory here is only over 3,000 jars. Recently, the price opened at 37 yuan to 34 yuan. The shop inventory is even lower, approximately 2,000 jars. The current sales are still good, with the wholesale price at 36 yuan and the subsequent price at 32 yuan. The trend is stable.

Silk and Tea: Overseas Silk Prices Not High 192

Yesterday, the silk market of foreign firms in this port still showed no upward trend. The silk weaving factories in Lyon are currently trying to reduce costs, and silk prices are not high. The telegram price is small, and European firms are also hoping to hoard at low prices, making transactions difficult. Yesterday, only Xinfu and others brought in 30 bales of Shanghai white factory silk, and Dachang brought in 10 bales of white dry silk. Prices were both firm, it was said.

Italian Raw Silk Turns Higher 193

Since the new silk season began in the Milan market, sales in Europe and the United States have not improved. Silk prices have gradually declined. Recently, due to the nationwide earthquake, there is no hope for autumn silkworms, and Italian silk has gradually turned higher. The sales of Double Special grade to France has slightly moved, with the price rising by 3 lire, and the price of Special grade rising by 2 lire, it was said.

Ping Shui's Big Firms Active in US Sales 194

Yesterday, the tea market in this port saw a trend of active sales from US firms. Jinlong, Yihuo, and other firms, as well as the China Tea Company, have all begun operations. However, with silver prices low by two to three taels, several large firms on the main road are also in negotiations. Gongxi green tea from the Russian Cooperative Association and Baitou Zhuang have large purchases, and transactions are not sluggish. Yihuo, Xiehe, and other firms also have a high demand for Zhenmei and Xiumei. The above-mentioned green teas are not difficult to sell. Only Zhenmei remains sluggish in the market. The recent hoarding is visibly abundant, which is a concern for tea merchants, it was said.

Hardware: This Factory's Wire Nail Sales Are Stagnant 195

This factory's wire nails were very prosperous in Henan and Shanxi in the past. There were negotiations and inquiries almost every day. Recently, due to the uncertainty of the war, those groups have not been inquiring, and the market is very cold. The Hankou and inland groups are also unable to calculate profits due to the high bottom prices, so there are very few transactions, almost as rare as stars in the morning. The current market price is 6 taels 1 qian and a half per barrel. According to an investigation by various dealers exclusively distributed by Quan Shen, the current daily sales volume is only about 270-280 barrels. This situation is truly the cold era for this factory's nails.

Hardware Market Trends Higher with Exchange Rates 196

With foreign exchange rates continuously declining in recent days, the cost of various hardware goods has quietly increased significantly. Therefore, various dealers have again discussed raising prices in order to maintain the market and make up for the losses. As a result, the market sentiment is good, and everyone is raising their buying prices by two to three qian. Customer deliveries will also begin in the coming days, so the market trend is very optimistic.

Kelun Hospital Specializes in Treating Venereal Diseases 276

Venereal diseases are terrible and frightening, lurking within the human body and breaking out when the opportunity arises. During this hot and humid weather, syphilis, chancroid, gonorrhea, buboes, and fish mouth are rampant. Every year, every month, and even every day, countless people lose their lives, and even more pass it on to future generations. This invisible killer is far more devastating than visible water, fire, knives, and weapons. Unfortunately, people often fail to notice and indulge in sensual pleasures. Once infected with venereal disease, they are careless and unaware of the need to eradicate it early. By the time the poison has deeply accumulated and the limbs are crippled, they are shocked and seek medical treatment, but they do not know how to choose a doctor, resulting in being harmed by quacks, which is very pitiful. Kelun Hospital (opposite the Far East Hotel on Xizang Road), in view of this, for the sake of personal happiness, for the sake of social health, and for the development of the entire nation, loudly calls out and specifically warns patients not to avoid medical treatment and to quickly come to this hospital for diagnosis and treatment. However, patients often do not know the symptoms and signs of the disease, so we have specially described the various symptoms and harms of venereal diseases in detail below, so that readers know and patients know how to seek medical treatment and choose a doctor, so as not to disappoint the hospital's careful warning.

(Syphilis) Initially, only small hard nodules, redness, swelling, and ulceration appear on the glans (or on the labia majora and minora in women). This stony hard nodule is called a hard chancre. At this time, the bacteria have not yet spread. After a few days, buboes appear between the hips, with hard swelling and slight pain, indicating that the bacteria have gradually entered the whole body through the blood vessels. This is the first stage of symptoms. If you do not seek treatment immediately, the spread will become more extensive and reach the terrible second stage. At this time, the whole body is weak, the joints are sore, red rashes appear on the face and body, sore throat, red eyes, headache, stomach pain are present, it is worse at night, hair falls out, and the nails become deformed. If treatment is not appropriate, it will turn into a dangerous third stage. In the third stage, the internal organs rot, rubbery tumors appear all over the body, the limbs are paralyzed, the voice is hoarse, the eyes are blind, the ears are deaf, and the bridge of the nose collapses, leading to death. The cruel state is difficult to describe in writing. Our hospital uses various scientific methods to treat this disease and is responsible for eradicating it. In addition to using 606, 914 and other injections, we also use the latest invented secret agent sulfonamide and other methods to completely eradicate syphilis of any stage in the shortest period of time, ensuring that the blood test will never have after-effects.

(Gonorrhea) is the most common venereal disease, but it is also the most difficult venereal disease to eradicate. Treatment is often ineffective, lasting for many years, causing lifelong harm and hindering reproduction. This disease initially only secretes a kind of pus from the urethral opening, and patients often do not pay much attention to it. Later, the pain gradually increases and even bleeding occurs, and then they panic and seek medical treatment, but they do not know that it has become a serious acute gonorrhea. If the treatment is still not appropriate, orchitis, prostatitis, gonorrheal arthritis, gonorrheal eye disease, etc. will inevitably occur, which can damage the internal organs and harm the five senses, and also turn acute gonorrhea into chronic gonorrhea. Not only are specialists available, but it can also be guaranteed that there will be no obstacles to fertility. Initially, white turbidity reduces in three hours, pain stops in seven days and recovery occurs. Chronic old white turbidity is eradicated in two weeks and will never recur.

(Chancroid) is divided into hard and soft chancroid. Hard chancre is the initial stage of syphilis. Soft chancre is the most serious local disease of the genitals. Initially, men develop a white ulcer on the penis, and women develop it on the labia, secreting pus and causing pain, and the ulcer becomes larger and larger until it is uncontrollable, even to the point of rotting away the entire reproductive organ. The pain and cruelty are unmatched. Our hospital uses a new scientific injection method that can immediately relieve the pain after one injection and achieve success in three to five days, ensuring no after-effects. We dare to say that it is the only effective treatment for chancroid and is definitely not comparable to those who boast without knowledge.

(Buboes and Fish Mouth) Buboes mostly occur with syphilis, gonorrhea, chancroid, etc. Those that initially occur with syphilis are painless buboes. Thereafter, they gradually swell and become larger, the pain gradually increases, and walking becomes difficult. If the disease progresses further, it will suppurate and break, with pus and blood dripping out, and its shape is like a fish opening its mouth, hence the name fish mouth. Although this disease comes on quickly, it is very slow to heal, and the pain suffered by the patient is more severe than any other external disease. The medical method of our hospital is different from others and can definitely relieve the pain with one injection and achieve success with three injections. Art World

The Recent Turkish Literary Scene 明· 278

Because the Turkish Republic government is striving for national rejuvenation, it has gradually awakened many long-dormant activities. Therefore, it is expected that Turkish literature will soon become very active. At present, efforts in this area are still mediocre, but such efforts can be said to be the beginning of better harvests. It can be asserted that a country like Turkey will definitely produce good literature. This ancient country in the Near East has a beautiful and dramatic historical background, filled with colorful legends and folk literature, which are the materials for excellent national literature, although the Turks still do not value their treasure of folk literature.

However, the inability of Turkish literature to develop also has its reasons. Because if Turkey wants to make its literature flourish, it must first solve the significant problem of illiteracy. Currently, there are five million people in Turkey who cannot read or write. The government's current universal education movement provides some basic education to 500,000 adults each year, but even at this rate, the huge project of the "literacy movement" cannot be completed in less than ten years.

Since Turkey adopted the Latin alphabet more than a year ago, more than 1,000 books have been printed using the new phonetic spelling method, 80% of which are school textbooks. In addition, in terms of literature, there are 40 novels, 30 collections of children's stories, and 15 collections of poems. As for the number of writers, although it is said that it has increased since the abolition of the Arabic script, they cannot find publishers because of the difficulty in selling new phonetic spelling books. For example, for novels, the sales of old-style writing were already not good. The number of copies printed for each type is probably from 200 to 2,000, but very few can sell more than 500 copies. "The Wren" by Reshad Nouri is a Turkish book,

The Best-Selling Book 279

Since its first publication in his youth, it has sold about 25,000 copies so far, but this book has never been reprinted in the new script because reprinting it in the new script would mean no sales.

Therefore, writers have repeatedly asked the government to provide some subsidies to encourage the construction of new literature, but the government has always refused. However, the Turkish Ministry of Education has recently contacted the French Hachette bookstore and agreed to provide financial assistance from the government in the first year if the bookstore can add management offices for selling books, magazines, and newspapers throughout Turkey. The purpose of this plan is to expand the sales of books because, at present, the Turkish reading community is completely concentrated in the big cities. 80% of Turkish books are absorbed by the four major cities: Istanbul accounts for 30%, Ankara accounts for 25%, Smyrna accounts for 20%, and Samsun accounts for 10%. The remaining 20% is scattered in three small cities.

The book business is still mostly based on books printed in Arabic script. There are still inventories of this type of book. As for books in the new script, sales are really not great because the older generation, who read for entertainment, would rather look at the old-style script. Only students are used to reading books in the new script. However, a new Turkish dictionary has recently been published, containing 30,000 new script words spelled with Latin letters. This dictionary is certainly very useful.

Because of the small number of literate people, the level of culture in Turkey has never been popular, so the publishing industry in Turkey has never been developed. The bookstores are full of dusty pamphlets, which are printed using a stencil duplicator method. Each page is inserted with meticulous brush paintings, like Persian miniature religious paintings. And because of the shortage of paper, paper is used very economically. The densely packed text of each book is diagonally written on the bottom edge of each page, making the words in a book messy, and unclear. These books are bound with soft paper covers, and each book sells for about one or two dimes. All the old-style novels in Turkey are printed like this, and these novels are well-known and almost memorized by everyone, such as "The Minstrel," "Shayi Si Mei" (SbabIsmaiI) "The Minstrel You Mo" (EumertbeMinatrel) "Jiu Luo Qiao" (Kiucogion) "Lena and Medlong" (LeyIaandMedjooun), "Jilin and Ashley" (keremandAsli), etc. The status of these books in Turkey is the same as "Bishenghua," "Zaishengyuan," "Zhengdong," "Zhengxi," "Yu Qingting," and "Shuangzhufeng" in our China.

But this traditional literature is now greatly declining. Compared with those new-style novels that have been published in the past few years, the sales volume is quite different. However, most of these new-style novels are imitations of European romance novels. The structure is ordinary, the content is superficial, and they have no literary value. Moreover, these novels are often published in newspapers day by day, so they are procrastinating, lengthy, and tasteless, which is similar to our newspaper novels.

There are no outstanding figures among Turkish modern novelists. 280

Hussein Rahmi, Hassan Djemal, and Reshad Nouri all have a portion of readers, and their influence is comparable. Among Turkish novels that have been translated into foreign languages, only "The Wren" has been translated into German. Reshad Nouri (the author of "The Wren") is popular because of his simple style, which is simple and natural, without the traces of Persian-Arabic influence, and is indeed unique.

"The Wren" 281

is the story of a girl, Meride, who, because she was angered by her fiancé, ran away to Anatolia to teach. The tone of this novel is very slow. It describes in detail Meride's childhood and teaching experience. The monotonous and silent life in the Anatolian countryside is like a vivid picture unfolded between the pages of this book. At the end, Meride returned to Istanbul and married her lover. The author, Reshad Nouri, is a prolific novelist. Among his famous novels are "From Lips to Heart," "Stain," and "Secret Hands."

In the Near East, modern romance novels have replaced ancient mysterious literature. Only those scholars are working hard to preserve the philosophical texts and poems of ancient monks and hermits, because these things have become antiques. As for the tastes of the Turkish reading community, that can be measured by looking at one thing. Among the foreign literature translations in Turkey, the most popular is Zola's "Loyalty" (Verjte), and "Loyalty" is a very "romantic and sensual" novel.

Many Western literary classics have been translated using new letters because European literature is welcomed by a large number of people in Turkey, and this is indeed a commendable thing because the introduction of European literature will undoubtedly have a good influence on the Turkish literary scene. As for Turkish folk tales, because they have been passed down from generation to generation for hundreds of years, very few have been printed into books. Even if there are, they are only printed into the kind of pamphlets mentioned above. Naseddirl Kbodja, a comedian from the era of Emperor Timur, is luckier than others in folk legends. A pamphlet of 80 pages, recounting his life deeds, has recently been published, tracing his childhood, student days, youth, the era of being a judge, and the era of old age. Last year, a bookstore in Turkey printed a book in new letters, dedicated to the stories of this comedian and fabulist. However, there are really too many of his stories in the legend. This is only a very small part of them.

There is also a very familiar figure in Turkish folk literature, 282

Karagoz. Legends about him will also be preserved in the same way. The person doing this work is Professor Selim Bey of Robert College. The stories of this famous figure, in addition to being written into puppet show scripts, have never been printed. Only a German oriental scholar, Doctor Rettor, published a well-printed illustrated book a few years ago, which collected several puppet show scripts centered on Karagoz, but that was not purely "Karagoz stories." Selim Bey's goal is to record the Karagoz stories of folk legends without modification, so it can be considered an important work in Turkish folklore. It is only a pity that, in order to facilitate popularity, the editor tried his best to eliminate these

Page 18

obscenities in the stories, so that it would not be offensive and would not hinder the spread, but the true face of these stories was therefore cut off in part. Karagoz was a comedian who lived in the era of Sultan Orhan, who did many strange things and later became a famous figure in legends. (To be continued)

World Artists Coming to Shanghai Soon Wei· 283

A. Strok, a foreign resident in Shanghai, travels to Europe and the United States every year to contact and sign contracts with famous modern artists, introducing them to perform in major cities in the Far East. Over the years, he has successively introduced John McCormack, Jascba Heifetz, Mischa Elman, Ruth St. Denis, La Argentina, etc. This spring, he made another trip to Europe and returned to Shanghai last week. He has contacted and signed many modern musicians, singers, and dancers who will come to the Far East one after another, and Shanghai is the first place they will arrive. Mr. Si is an old friend of many years, and yesterday I specially visited his residence to talk about everything. Now, I will briefly describe the artists who are coming to Shanghai soon as obtained from the conversation and report to the readers.

(1) Sakharoff Dancers. This troupe is currently performing in major cities in Europe such as Paris, Berlin, and London. It is one of the most outstanding modern dance troupes. Its artistic reputation is no less than that of Povloua, Denicoaun, La Argentina, and other dancers.

(2) Singers Toti Dal Monte and Muro Lomanto will come to Shanghai together. The former is a soprano singer, and the latter is a baritone singer. When they come to Shanghai, they will join a large string orchestra to perform.

(3) Jovita Fuente is a modern female soprano singer who has enjoyed honors in major cities such as Berlin, Milan, and Paris. She is already on her way and will arrive in Japan soon.

(4) Tito Scbipa is a famous Italian baritone singer who has recorded many Victor discs and is very famous in Europe and the United States.

(5) Elrem Zimbalist, a modern violin master, is coming to Shanghai to perform soon.

(6) Heifetz is a modern violin king, who doesn't know him? He originally planned to come to Shanghai last year, but he stopped because he was afraid of the situation. He will definitely come as scheduled next year.

(7) Kreisler is also a famous violinist, as famous as Heifetz. He will come after Mr. Ha.

(8) Sergei Rachmaninoff is a famous modern pianist who has composed many famous pieces in his life.

In addition, all the artists from La Scala Theater in Milan, a world-famous theater, will come to cooperate in a grand drama performance.

Art World Manuscript Regulations 284

(1) Articles should be limited to news, reviews, and introductions about recent art (painting, music, sculpture, architecture, drama, etc.) and literature at home and abroad.

(2) Photos should be limited to recent portraits of domestic and foreign writers and their works, and various photographs related to the articles.

(3) The number of words in each article should not exceed 2,000.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) Do not write manuscripts horizontally, do not write carelessly, and Western texts can be omitted. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(6) Do not draw illustrations in manuscripts with blue ink, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black ink.

(7) Please indicate that the manuscript is for the Art World Department.

(8) Manuscripts will not be returned whether or not they are published. If a return is required, it must be stated in advance and sufficient postage stamps must be attached.

(9) Remuneration for articles is four yuan, three yuan, and two yuan per thousand words. The same applies to pictures and photos per piece. Special manuscripts will be remunerated separately.

Book and Newspaper Introductions

Hanging Branches Tune - Li · Substitute · Hua · 285

I once said that "Bai Xue Yi Yin Continued Selection" is a very good collection of folk songs. Now, the "Hanging Branches Tune" I'm about to discuss is also a book of equal value.

"Hanging Branches Tune" contains forty-one folk love songs, and it is said to be the work of Feng Youlong, a talented and uninhibited man of the Chongzhen period of the Ming Dynasty. However, some people doubt who the author really is. Zheng Zhenduo once cited a passage from Shen Defu's "Gu Qu Za Yan" to prove that "Hanging Branches Tune" was not created by Feng, but was actually one of the popular folk songs. Shen Defu's "Gu Qu Za Yan" says:

During the Jiajing and Longqing periods (嘉隆間), the practice of singing "Wu Geng" (五更) and "Yin Jiao Si" (銀絞絲) became popular. From the Huai River region to Jiangnan, it gradually drifted away from Ci and Qu poetry, only depicting lewd and obscene situations, with a slight variation in tone. In recent years, there have been two more tunes, "Da Zao Gan" (打棗乾) and "Hanging Branches Tune" (掛枝兒), whose melodies are roughly similar. Therefore, regardless of north or south, male or female, old or young, noble or lowly, everyone learns them and enjoys listening to them. They have even been published in volumes and are recited all over the world, deeply touching people's hearts. No one knows where the scores come from, which is truly astonishing.

From this perspective, the claim that Feng created it seems difficult to establish. Moreover, from another perspective, Feng Youlong was originally someone who liked to revise the works of others, such as "Liang Jiang Ji" (量江記) and "Yi Peng Xue" (一捧雪) (renamed "Feng Liu Meng" 風流夢), which, together with over ten other plays in "Mo Han Zhai Chuan Qi" (墨憨齋傳奇), added "Ping Yao Zhuan" (平妖傳) and other novels, such as "Zhi Nang" (智囊), "Qing Shi" (情史), "Xing Shi Heng Yan" (醒世恒言), "Jing Shi Tong Yan" (警世通言), "Yu Shi Ming Yan" (喩世明言), etc., were all proofread and adapted by him. As for the forty-one love songs in "Hanging Branches Tune," their exquisite beauty is naturally unmatched by purely folk songs. It is evident that they have been embellished by the hands of scholars. Therefore, it is more believable to say that "Hanging Branches Tune" was originally a folk song, collected and modified by Feng.

Although "Hanging Branches Tune" and "Bai Xue Yi Yin Continued Selection" both sing about the affairs of men and women, "Hanging Branches Tune" is more subtle and implicit in its depictions of sexual desire and kissing and hugging than "Bai Xue Yi Yin Continued Selection." For example, even when the book describes more direct flirting, it is not crude:

Darling, I care about you so much, I wish I could swallow you into my stomach with a bowl of water. I think about you every day, I long for you every day, but it's no use. I pluck up the courage to kiss you, thank goodness, you don't refuse. If I had known you wouldn't refuse, why did I wait until today to do this?

Flirting (1)

Compared with songs like "Lover Loves Me," "Jade Beauty," and "Happy to Be Happy" in "Bai Xue Yi Yin Continued Selection," this is naturally much more nuanced and delicate. As for "I wish I could swallow you into my stomach with a gulp of water," this is a purely folk saying that is very popular. I remember hearing a tune like this:

Oh, my, oh, my, when I was little, I looked like an ugly pig. I can't sleep at midnight or in the early morning. I think of it, during the day, the handsome young man passes by the door. He passes by the door, and a mouthful of cold water goes down my stomach.

As for whether she later plucked up the courage to kiss him like in the flirting song, I unfortunately didn't hear the end. However, I always feel that many folk songs are similar to this. Moreover, the more popular a folk song is, the more different it is in different regions. However, these differences are not completely different in their main points. Instead, due to local customs and dialects, they are different on the surface but similar in essence. When we compare and study this "Hanging Branches Tune" with "Bai Xue Yi Yin Continued Selection," we find that several songs are the same. It can be clearly seen that they originated from the same source. Here are some examples:

The pretty girl points her finger at Du Kang and scolds him, you made wine because of beauty, and made me, the wronged one, drunk. You come in and fall into my arms, regardless of who sees you, luckily my husband is not at home. Oh, you greedy-for-beauty and fond-of-wine wronged one, you treat your life as a joke.

| Scolding Du Kang (Hanging Branches Tune)

I hate it so much I want to scold Du Kang, he made the fine wine and made the wronged one drunk. He got so drunk that he talked nonsense and scolded me. He couldn't stand still and bumped into my arms. I'm glad my husband isn't home. If he were home, this mess would be bigger than the sky. Call, lover, take a lantern and go back.

| Hating to Start (Bai Xue Yi Yin Continued Selection)

Melon seeds are not rare, wrapped in a handkerchief and given to my dear brother. Each one has been on the tip of my tongue. The gift is light, but the meaning is heavy, good things don't need to be many. Please give my best regards to my dear brother, and don't forget me.

| Giving Melon Seeds (Hanging Branches Tune)

Melon seeds are not a rare item, wrapped in paper and handkerchief, and given to my dear lover. Good ones don't need many, one is equal to one, and each one has been on the tip of my tongue. I advise my lover to eat them, and don't forget me, don't forget me.

| Melon Seeds (Bai Xue Yi Yin Continued Selection)

Therefore, when we study folk songs, if we can work hard to collect and compare the slightly different versions from various regions, we will surely increase our interest and make more new discoveries. Moreover, we can see their original faces. However, many of those who collect folk songs still only know how to select one or two of the better ones from the many slightly different songs and consider themselves satisfied. The rest are discarded like worn-out shoes and are not cared about. In this way, there will be no good results for folk songs. Furthermore, the collection of folk ballads and stories may also have this problem. I hope that those who work hard in folk literature will recognize this point.

"Hanging Branches Tune" has more songs about objects than "Bai Xue Yi Yin Continued Selection." Among the forty-one songs, there are as many as seven: "Lotus Dewdrop," "Zongzi," "Mirror," "Golden Needle," "Bound Feet," "Curtain Hook," and "Xiao." However, each song contains subtle and intricate double meanings, which are extremely interesting. For example:

Lotus dewdrop, the precious leaves reveal my infatuated heart, using thread to string them together. Who knew you would be so fickle, scattering here and there and gathering there. Oh, you heartless wronged one, following the wind and turning.

This way of expressing one's emotions through singing about objects is so natural and so moving. Let's look at this song about the golden needle, which uses hidden metaphors in its words:

Golden needle, I love you with all my heart, hoping to thread you through. How can you know, when we meet occasionally, how can I bear to abandon you? I often tease you, don't you think your heart is made of iron?

If only a thread could connect, it would not be in vain to work with you.

This kind of game of using "needle" (針) to imply "truth" (眞) and "sew" (縫) to imply "meet" (逢) has always been very popular in China. For example, in ancient poems, "hibiscus" (芙蓉) implies "husband's face" (夫容), "lotus" (蓮) implies "pity" (憐), "silk" (絲) implies "thought" (思), and "tombstone" (碑) implies "sadness" (悲). In addition, there are many examples in Liu Yuxi's "Bamboo Branch Song," such as "The sun rises in the east and rain falls in the west, it is said to be cloudless but there is love" (東邊日出西邊雨、道是無晴却有晴), where "cloudless" (晴) implies "love" (情). As for songs and ballads, there are even more uses of hidden metaphors. For example, in the Cantonese folk song, "After the rain, the spider still spins its web, wanting sunshine, one can only think in secret" (雨後蜘蛛還結網、想晴惟有暗中思), "sunshine" (晴) implies "love" (情), and "silk" (絲) implies "thought" (思), which is a very good example. In short, this kind of metaphorical comparison always uses the borrowing of objects or the similarity of sounds to express inner emotions.

Finally, I feel that folk literature is the crystallization of national thought and the expression of the common heart of a nation. It expresses the characteristics and national spirit of this nation. At the same time, it allows us to see its strengths and weaknesses, and to reform, enlighten, guide, and support them, so that they can reach a glorious and splendid realm day by day.
